bYWHwf">Cancer Council South Australia acknowledges and pays respect to the Traditional Owners of the lands and waterways on which we live and work. We extend that respect to all Elders, past and present, as well as all other Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Peoples. Cancer Council SA recognises that improved cancer outcomes are more likely to be achieved when Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Peoples have a say in matters that affect them.<br>
We acknowledge that Aboriginal & Torres Strait Islander Peoples have a unique spiritual connection to Country and we are committed to reconciliation and embedding this in the culture and operations of Cancer Council SA.
